            const country = geo.country.toUpperCase();
            const region = geo.region.toUpperCase();

            if (!shouldLoadOneTrustScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region)) {
                return;
            }

            preloadBannerSdk();

            ONE_TRUST_LIBRARIES.forEach((library) => {
                loadScript(library.url, "text/javascript", library.options);
            });

            if (country === "US") {
                loadCCPAAddon();
            }
        }

        // VARIABLE EXAMPLE
        // countriesWithOneTrustEnabled = {
        //     "countries": ["TR","PL"],
        //     "regions": ["CA","NY"]
        // }

        function shouldLoadOneTrustScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) {
            if (!countriesWithOneTrustEnabled || Object.keys(countriesWithOneTrustEnabled).length === 0) {
                return false;
            }

            if (country === 'US') {
                const regionsToLoad = countriesWithOneTrustEnabled.regions;

                if (Array.isArray(regionsToLoad) && regionsToLoad.length > 0) {
                    if (regionsToLoad.includes(region)) {
                        return true;
                    }
                }
            }

            const countriesToLoad = countriesWithOneTrustEnabled.countries;

            if (Array.isArray(countriesToLoad) && countriesToLoad.length > 0) {
                return countriesToLoad.includes(country);
            }
        }

        function loadScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = createScript(url, type, options);

            document.head.appendChild(script);
        }

        function createScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = document.createElement("script");

            script.src = url;
            script.type = type;
            script.async = true;

            for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(options)) {
                script.setAttribute(key, value);
            }

            script.setAttribute("data-domain-script", DATA_DOMAIN_SCRIPT);

            return script;
        }

        function loadCCPAAddon() {
            loadScript(CCPA_ADDON.url, "text/javascript", CCPA_ADDON.options);
        }

        function preloadBannerSdk() {
            const link = document.createElement("link");
            link.href = BANNER_SDK.url;
            link.rel = "preload";
            link.as = "script";

            document.head.appendChild(link);
        }

        function oneTrustLoaded() {
            return !!(window.OneTrust || window.OneTrustStub);
        }

        console.debug('OneTrust setup', countriesWithOneTrustEnabled);

        function waitForGeo() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                let counter = 0;
                const maxCount = 10;
                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    const geo = getGeo();
                    if (geo || counter >= maxCount) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        resolve(geo);
                    }
                    counter++;
                }, 100);
            });
        }

        async function waitForGeoAndLoadScripts() {
            const geo = await waitForGeo();
            if (geo && !oneTrustLoaded()) {
                loadOneTrustScripts(geo);
            }
        }

        if (!oneTrustLoaded()) {
            const geo = getGeo();

            if (geo) {
                loadOneTrustScripts(geo);
            } else {
                waitForGeoAndLoadScripts();
            }
        }
    })();
</script>

<script>
    (function () {
        function shouldLoadKetchScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) {
            const countriesWithKetchEnabled = {"countries":["IN","HU","SG"]};
            if (!countriesWithKetchEnabled || Object.keys(countriesWithKetchEnabled).length === 0) {
                return false;
            }
            const countriesToLoad = countriesWithKetchEnabled.countries;

            if (Array.isArray(countriesToLoad) && countriesToLoad.length > 0) {
                return countriesToLoad.includes(country);
            }
        }


        function loadKetchScripts(geo) {
            const country = geo.country.toUpperCase();
            const region = geo.region.toUpperCase();
            if (!shouldLoadKetchScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region)) {
                return;
            }

            window.semaphore = window.semaphore || [];

            window.ketch = function () {
                window.semaphore.push(arguments);
            };

            var urlParams = new URLSearchParams(document.location.search);
            var property = urlParams.has("property") ? urlParams.get("property") : "website_smart_tag";

            var scriptElement = document.createElement("script");
            scriptElement.type = "text/javascript";
            scriptElement.src = "https://global.ketchcdn.com/web/v2/config/fandom/" + property + "/boot.js";
            scriptElement.defer = scriptElement.async = true;

            document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(scriptElement);
        }

        function ketchLoaded() {
            return !!window.ketch;
        }

        function getCookieValue(cookieName) {
            const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
            return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
        }

        function getGeo() {
            try {
                return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo')));
            } catch {
                return null;
            }
        }

        function waitForGeo() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                let counter = 0;
                const maxCount = 10;
                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    const geo = getGeo();
                    if (geo || counter >= maxCount) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        resolve(geo);
                    }
                    counter++;
                }, 100);
            });
        }

        async function waitForGeoAndLoadScripts() {
            const geo = await waitForGeo();
            if (geo && !ketchLoaded()) {
                loadKetchScripts(geo);
            }
        }

        if (!ketchLoaded()) {
            const geo = getGeo();

            if (geo) {
                loadKetchScripts(geo);
            } else {
                waitForGeoAndLoadScripts();
            }
        }
    })();
</script>

<script>
    (async function () {
        // const AIRGAP_URL = '<script
        // data-cfasync="false"
        // src=""
        const AIRGAP_URL = 'https://transcend-cdn.com/cm/54b0c313-5d22-47e5-92fd-f979a37d1ad0/airgap.js';
        const countriesWithAirgapEnabled = [];

        function getCookieValue(cookieName) {

            const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
            return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
        }

        function getGeo() {
            try {
                return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo')));
            } catch {
                return null;
            }
        }

        function loadAirgapScripts(geo) {
            const country = geo.country.toUpperCase();
            const region = geo.region.toUpperCase();
            const enabled = shouldLoadAirgapScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) || airgapScriptForced();

            if (!enabled) {
                return;
            }

            loadScript(AIRGAP_URL, "text/javascript", {
                'data-cfasync': false
            });
        }

        // VARIABLE EXAMPLE
        // countriesWithAirgapEnabled = {
        //     "countries": ["TR","PL"],
        //     "regions": ["CA","NY"]
        // }

        function airgapScriptForced() {
            return window.location.search.includes('icPreferredCMP=airgap');
        }

        function shouldLoadAirgapScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) {
            if (!countriesWithAirgapEnabled || Object.keys(countriesWithAirgapEnabled).length === 0) {
                return false;
            }

            if (country === 'US') {
                const regionsToLoad = countriesWithAirgapEnabled.regions;

                if (Array.isArray(regionsToLoad) && regionsToLoad.length > 0) {
                    if (regionsToLoad.includes(region)) {
                        return true;
                    }
                }
            }

            const countriesToLoad = countriesWithAirgapEnabled.countries;

            if (Array.isArray(countriesToLoad) && countriesToLoad.length > 0) {
                return countriesToLoad.includes(country);
            }
        }

        function loadScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = createScript(url, type, options);

            document.head.appendChild(script);
        }

        function createScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = document.createElement("script");

            script.src = url;
            script.type = type;
            script.async = true;

            for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(options)) {
                script.setAttribute(key, value);
            }

            return script;
        }

        console.debug('Airgap setup', countriesWithAirgapEnabled);

        function waitForGeo() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                let counter = 0;
                const maxCount = 10;
                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    const geo = getGeo();
                    if (geo || counter >= maxCount) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        resolve(geo);
                    }
                    counter++;
                }, 100);
            });
        }

        let geo = getGeo();

        if (geo === null) {
            geo = await waitForGeo();
        }

        if (geo) {
            loadAirgapScripts(geo);
        }
    })();
</script>

<script>
	const useMaxDefaultContentWidth = Boolean(false);

	const defaultContentWidth = useMaxDefaultContentWidth ? 'expanded' : 'collapsed';

	let contentWidthPreference;

	try {
		contentWidthPreference = localStorage.getItem('contentwidth') || defaultContentWidth;
	} catch (e) {
		contentWidthPreference = defaultContentWidth;
	}

	if ( contentWidthPreference === 'expanded' ) {
		document.documentElement.classList.add('is-content-expanded');
	}
</script>

													<script data-name="featured-video-mapped-to-wiki">
	(function () {
		// we can't use mw.config here because it's too early so we need to pass this data in different way
		const videoDetails = {
			mapping: {"mediaId":"sXWp3rZ0","connatixPlaylistId":"36081eca-e784-4e30-87c3-133cf673e447","impressionsPerSession":4},
			impressionsPerSession: 4,
		};
		const videoBridgeCountries = ["AE","AG","AL","AM","AR","AT","AU","AZ","BA","BB","BD","BG","BH","BN","BO","BR","BS","BY","CA","CH","CL","CN","CO","CR","CU","CY","CZ","DE","DK","DO","DZ","EC","EE","EG","ES","FI","FR","GB","GE","GF","GG","GH","GP","GR","GT","GU","GY","HK","HN","HR","HU","ID","IE","IL","IM","IN","IQ","IR","IS","IT","JE","JM","JO","JP","KE","KG","KH","KR","KW","KY","KZ","LA","LB","LK","LT","LU","LV","LY","MA","MD","ME","MK","MM","MN","MO","MQ","MT","MU","MV","MX","MY","NG","NI","NO","NP","NZ","OM","PA","PE","PH","PK","PL","PR","PS","PT","PY","QA","RE","RO","RS","RU","SA","SC","SE","SG","SI","SK","SV","TD","TH","TN","TR","TT","TW","UA","US","UY","UZ","VE","VI","VN","ZA","ZW"];
		const tier3VideoBridgeCountries = ["GB","BE","NL","DE","AU","MX","AR","FR","MD","CA","ES","IT","PE","CO","CL","NZ"];
		let hasVideoOnPage = null;

		function getCookieValue(cookieName) {
			const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
			return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
		}

		function hasMaxedOutPlayerImpressionsInWiki() {
			const impressionsSoFar = Number(getCookieValue('playerImpressionsInWiki')) || 0;
			const allowedImpressions = Number(videoDetails.impressionsPerSession);

			return impressionsSoFar >= allowedImpressions;
		}

		function getCountryCode() {
			try {
				return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo'))).country.toLowerCase();
			} catch {
				return null;
			}
		}

		function isVideoBridgeAllowedForCountry() {
			const countryCode = getCountryCode();

			if (!countryCode) {
				return false;
			}

			// If it's a default mapping, then check the country whitelist from the default mapping.
			if (videoDetails?.mapping?.isDefaultMapping) {
				// If the wiki is classified as a tier3 wiki, then check the country whitelist from the tier3VideoBridge whitelist.
				const allowedCountriesForTier3Wikis = tier3VideoBridgeCountries.map(function (allowedTier3CountryCode) {
					return allowedTier3CountryCode.toLowerCase();
				})

				return allowedCountriesForTier3Wikis.indexOf(countryCode) !== -1;
			} else {
				// If not a default mapping wiki (so it's a wiki mapping), then check the country whitelist from the videoBridge whitelist
				const allowedCountries = videoBridgeCountries.map(function (allowedCountryCode) {
					return allowedCountryCode.toLowerCase();
				});

				return allowedCountries.indexOf(countryCode) !== -1;
			}
		}

		window.fandomIsVideoPossible = function () {
			if (hasVideoOnPage === null) {
				hasVideoOnPage =
					videoDetails.mapping &&
					isVideoBridgeAllowedForCountry() &&
					!hasMaxedOutPlayerImpressionsInWiki();
			}

			return hasVideoOnPage;
		};

		window.canPlayVideo = function () {
			return window.fandomIsVideoPossible()
		};

		if (!window.canPlayVideo()) {
			document.body.classList.add('no-featured-video');
		} else {
			document.body.classList.add('has-featured-video');
		}
	})();
</script>

<section class="pi-item pi-group pi-border-color pi-collapse pi-collapse-open">
	<h2 class="pi-item pi-header pi-secondary-font pi-item-spacing pi-secondary-background"><span class="df-header">Devil Fruit</span></h2>

<div class="pi-item pi-data pi-item-spacing pi-border-color" data-source="dfname">
	
		<h3 class="pi-data-label pi-secondary-font">Japanese Name:</h3>
	
	<div class="pi-data-value pi-font"><a href="/wiki/Fuku_Fuku_no_Mi" title="Fuku Fuku no Mi">Fuku Fuku no Mi</a></div>
</div>

<div class="pi-item pi-data pi-item-spacing pi-border-color" data-source="dfename">
	
		<h3 class="pi-data-label pi-secondary-font">English Name:</h3>
	
	<div class="pi-data-value pi-font">Garb-Garb Jutsu (VIZ and Funimation);<br />Garb-Garb Fruit (One Piece Official YouTube Channel)<sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup></div>
</div>

<div class="pi-item pi-data pi-item-spacing pi-border-color" data-source="dfmeaning">
	
		<h3 class="pi-data-label pi-secondary-font">Meaning:</h3>
	
	<div class="pi-data-value pi-font">Clothing</div>
</div>

<div class="pi-item pi-data pi-item-spacing pi-border-color" data-source="dftype">
	
		<h3 class="pi-data-label pi-secondary-font">Type:</h3>
	
	<div class="pi-data-value pi-font"><a href="/wiki/Paramecia" title="Paramecia">Paramecia</a></div>
</div>

</section>
</aside>
</p><table class="nomobile dfbox mw-collapsible WanoCountryColors" style="color: var(--colorscheme-txt, var(--pi-txt-fallback));">
<tbody><tr><th class="cs" style="background: var(--colorscheme-bg, var(--pi-bg-fallback))">Devil Fruit</th></tr>
<tr><td><div class="pi-item pi-data pi-item-spacing pi-border-color" data-source="dfname"><span class="pi-data-label pi-secondary-font">Japanese Name:</span>
<div class="pi-data-value pi-font"><a href="/wiki/Fuku_Fuku_no_Mi" title="Fuku Fuku no Mi">Fuku Fuku no Mi</a></div></div></td></tr>
<tr><td><div class="pi-item pi-data pi-item-spacing pi-border-color" data-source="dfename"><span class="pi-data-label pi-secondary-font">English Name:</span>
<div class="pi-data-value pi-font">Garb-Garb Jutsu (VIZ and Funimation);<br />Garb-Garb Fruit (One Piece Official YouTube Channel)<sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup></div></div></td></tr>
<tr><td><div class="pi-item pi-data pi-item-spacing pi-border-color" data-source="dfmeaning"><span class="pi-data-label pi-secondary-font">Meaning:</span>
<div class="pi-data-value pi-font">Clothing</div></div></td></tr>
<tr><td><div class="pi-item pi-data pi-item-spacing pi-border-color" data-source="dftype"><span class="pi-data-label pi-secondary-font">Type:</span>
<div class="pi-data-value pi-font"><a href="/wiki/Paramecia" title="Paramecia">Paramecia</a></div></div></td></tr>
</tbody></table>
<p><b>"Foxfire Kin'emon"</b><sup id="cite_ref-intro_8-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-intro-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup> is a <a href="/wiki/Samurai" title="Samurai">samurai</a> from the region of <a href="/wiki/Kuri" title="Kuri">Kuri</a> in <a href="/wiki/Wano_Country" title="Wano Country">Wano Country</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-c657p15_5-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c657p15-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> a retainer of the <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Family" title="Kouzuki Family">Kouzuki Family</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-c816p13_2-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c816p13-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> the leader of the <a href="/wiki/Nine_Red_Scabbards" title="Nine Red Scabbards">Nine Red Scabbards</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-c932_4-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c932-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup> the husband of <a href="/wiki/Tsurujo" title="Tsurujo">Tsurujo</a>, and a former thug.<sup id="cite_ref-thug_12-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-thug-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> He was born 56 years before the present day, but traveled 20 years forward in time when he was 36 years old.<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_7-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Due to Wano Country having been taken over by <a href="/wiki/Kurozumi_Orochi" title="Kurozumi Orochi">Kurozumi Orochi</a>, an ally of <a href="/wiki/Kaidou" title="Kaidou">Kaidou</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Four_Emperors" title="Four Emperors">Four Emperors</a>, Kin'emon set out on a seafaring quest to recruit warriors for his cause, bringing alongside him his master, <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Momonosuke" title="Kouzuki Momonosuke">Kouzuki Momonosuke</a>, as well as two of <a href="/wiki/Kurozumi_Kanjuro" title="Kurozumi Kanjuro">his</a> <a href="/wiki/Raizo" title="Raizo">comrades</a>. After a series of misadventures, Kin'emon ended up on the island of <a href="/wiki/Punk_Hazard" title="Punk Hazard">Punk Hazard</a>, where he met and joined forces with the <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">Straw Hat Pirates</a>, posing as Momonosuke's father during the journey to <a href="/wiki/Zou" title="Zou">Zou</a>.
</p><p>He is one of the central allies of the Straw Hats during the <a href="/wiki/Dressrosa_Saga" title="Dressrosa Saga">Dressrosa</a>, <a href="/wiki/Whole_Cake_Island_Saga" title="Whole Cake Island Saga">Whole Cake Island</a> and <a href="/wiki/Wano_Country_Saga" title="Wano Country Saga">Wano Country</a> Sagas.<sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-c817p8_14-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c817p8-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup>
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Appearance">Appearance</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKin%2527emon%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D1&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Kin'emon's appearance matches the stereotype of samurai found in ancient Japan, with a black topknot and goatee.<sup id="cite_ref-c657p15_5-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c657p15-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> At 295&#160;cm (9'8"), he is taller than <a href="/wiki/Brook" title="Brook">Brook</a> who stands at 277&#160;cm (9'1").<sup id="cite_ref-intro_8-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-intro-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup> He is also quite muscular.<sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> His eyes are asymmetrical, with his right eye opening more than his left.<sup id="cite_ref-c657p15_5-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c657p15-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>His attire consists of a samurai gi that is black and white striped on the left side and orange on the right. Kept on the left side of his torso is a pair of katana with identical flame-patterned sheaths. For footwear, he wears simple geta sandals.<sup id="cite_ref-intro_8-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-intro-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>He has the crest of the <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Family" title="Kouzuki Family">Kouzuki Family</a> tattooed on his back.<sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Over 25 years ago, he had blonde hair and did not wear it in a top-knot. It was only after Kin'emon became a proper samurai that it started resembling his current hairstyle.<sup id="cite_ref-c943_17-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c943-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Gallery">Gallery</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKin%2527emon%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D2&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Main_Series">Main Series</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKin%2527emon%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D3&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div style="text-align: center; font-size: 0.7em; color: ; margin: 0.7em 0;"><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 127px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 127px; height: 127px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b5/Kin%27emon%27s_Manga_Color_Scheme.png/revision/latest?cb=20130806071941" class="image"><img alt="Kin&#39;emon&#39;s Manga Color Scheme" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b5/Kin%27emon%27s_Manga_Color_Scheme.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/105?cb=20130806071941" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="105" height="105" data-image-name="Kin&#39;emon&#39;s Manga Color Scheme.png" data-image-key="Kin%27emon%27s_Manga_Color_Scheme.png" data-relevant="1" /></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Kin'emon's color scheme in the manga.
</div></span><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 127px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 127px; height: 127px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7e/Kin%27emon_in_the_Digitally_Colored_Manga.png/revision/latest?cb=20211027003915" class="image"><img alt="Kin&#39;emon in the Digitally Colored Manga" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="52" height="105" data-image-name="Kin&#39;emon in the Digitally Colored Manga.png" data-image-key="Kin%27emon_in_the_Digitally_Colored_Manga.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7e/Kin%27emon_in_the_Digitally_Colored_Manga.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/52?cb=20211027003915" class="lazyload" /></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Kin'emon in the <a href="/wiki/Digitally_Colored_Manga" title="Digitally Colored Manga">Digitally Colored Manga</a>.

<div style="text-align: center; font-size: 0.7em; color: ; margin: 0.7em 0;"><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 127px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 127px; height: 127px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/43/Kinemon_Anime_Concept_Art.png/revision/latest?cb=20190926080815" class="image"><img alt="Kinemon Anime Concept Art" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="39" height="105" data-image-name="Kinemon Anime Concept Art.png" data-image-key="Kinemon_Anime_Concept_Art.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/43/Kinemon_Anime_Concept_Art.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/39?cb=20190926080815" class="lazyload" /></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Kin'emon's concept art from the anime.
</div></span><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 127px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 127px; height: 127px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c4/Kin%27emon_Special_Episode.png/revision/latest?cb=20231224034637" class="image"><img alt="Kin&#39;emon Special Episode" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="60" height="105" data-image-name="Kin&#39;emon Special Episode.png" data-image-key="Kin%27emon_Special_Episode.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c4/Kin%27emon_Special_Episode.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/60?cb=20231224034637" class="lazyload" /></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Kin'emon in <a href="/wiki/Special_Feature!_Momonosuke%27s_Path_to_Becoming_a_Great_Shogun" title="Special Feature! <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personality">Personality</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKin%2527emon%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D6&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>During his youth, Kin'emon was a rather brash and rude thug who partook in thievery and assault in order to get rich quickly. He was irresponsible with money, frequently falling into financial debt due to endless gambling and stealing from his childhood friend, <a href="/wiki/Tsurujo" title="Tsurujo">Tsurujo</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-thug_12-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-thug-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> At the time, he was seemingly fine with dying, ignoring Tsurujo's advice to leave his involvement with the <a href="/wiki/Yakuza" title="Yakuza">yakuza</a> and find a normal job otherwise he could get killed (he happily claimed no one would miss him). Still, he had a conscience, which acted once he witnessed the chaos and destruction caused by the <a href="/wiki/Mountain_God" title="Mountain God">Mountain God</a> due to his actions, especially after learning that Tsurujo, who had backed him all this time and suffered from the troubles he caused, had fallen victim to the gigantic beast.<sup id="cite_ref-c961p5-9_18-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c961p5-9-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> He was going to confess for his crime until <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Oden" title="Kouzuki Oden">Kouzuki Oden</a> stopped him.<sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Kin'emon already showed great courage and a desire to protect those dear to him in his early years, something that earned him recognition from Oden. After witnessing Oden taking the blame for  the <a href="/wiki/Mountain_God_Incident" title="Mountain God Incident">Mountain God Incident</a>, Kin'emon became a devout follower of the shogun's son, claiming that he would die for him. After being encouraged by Yasuie to reform himself for Oden's sake, Kin'emon adopted a proper samurai etiquette and a very old fashioned manner of speech.<sup id="cite_ref-c943_17-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c943-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup> Due to his reformed outlook, Kin'emon now expects women to walk three steps behind men and talk gracefully and quietly. He, on many occasions, referred to <a href="/wiki/Nami" title="Nami">Nami</a> as a shameless, violent and obscene woman due to her careless behavior and felt disgraced when he got hit on the head by her.<sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> 
</p><p>Kin'emon seems to follow the code of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bushido" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Bushido">bushido</a>, claiming he would commit suicide if he could, for the shame of being dismembered without dying. Even after being completely dismembered by a "<a href="/wiki/Ope_Ope_no_Mi" title="Ope Ope no Mi">mysterious ability</a>", Kin'emon still maintained his pride as a decapitated, talking head. Like Momonosuke, Kin'emon is very stubborn, constantly refusing the help of others and claiming he does not need it, while also denying conditions like hunger and pain out of warrior's pride. Only after nearly freezing to death did he finally forsake his pride and ask for help. Kin'emon is greatly honorable, bowing before Sanji for saving his torso (which was separated from him at the time) and thanking him for his help, stating that he was now indebted to him.<sup id="cite_ref-c672_21-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c672-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>As shown by his constant refusal to accept help from <a href="/wiki/Sanji" title="Sanji">Sanji</a> and own claims, he holds a strong dislike for all <a href="/wiki/Pirate" title="Pirate">pirates</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> This is most likely due to his master <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Oden" title="Kouzuki Oden">Kouzuki Oden</a>'s death at the hands of <a href="/wiki/Kaidou" title="Kaidou">Kaidou</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Beasts_Pirates" title="Beasts Pirates">Beasts Pirates</a>. Similarly, Kin'emon once stated that he cannot stand the sight of dragons due to Kaidou himself being a dragon <a href="/wiki/Zoan" title="Zoan">Zoan</a> <a href="/wiki/Devil_Fruit" title="Devil Fruit">Devil Fruit</a> user, considering them detestable creatures and violently harming one at <a href="/wiki/Punk_Hazard" title="Punk Hazard">Punk Hazard</a> as a result.<sup id="cite_ref-c682_23-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c682-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> He also seems to be very quick to judge things, believing Zoro to be the one who robbed Ryuma's grave after seeing his sword <a href="/wiki/Shusui" title="Shusui">Shusui</a>, a national treasure from his country, sheathed at his waist.<sup id="cite_ref-c699_24-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c699-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/5e/Kin%27emon%27s_Perverted_Personality.png/revision/latest?cb=20140916075657" class="image"><img alt="Kin&#39;emon&#39;s Perverted Personality" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="121" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Kin&#39;emon&#39;s Perverted Personality.png" data-image-key="Kin%27emon%27s_Perverted_Personality.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/5e/Kin%27emon%27s_Perverted_Personality.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20140916075657" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/5e/Kin%27emon%27s_Perverted_Personality.png/revision/latest?cb=20140916075657" class="image"><img alt="Kin&#39;emon&#39;s Perverted Personality" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/5e/Kin%27emon%27s_Perverted_Personality.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20140916075657" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="121" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Kin&#39;emon&#39;s Perverted Personality.png" data-image-key="Kin%27emon%27s_Perverted_Personality.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/5e/Kin%27emon%27s_Perverted_Personality.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20140916075657" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Kin%27emon%27s_Perverted_Personality.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kin'emon's reaction to Nami's cleavage.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Kin'emon has a tendency to be quite perverted in spite of his sexist ideals. Though he seemed to be outraged at Nami's sense of fashion, he still greatly enjoyed ogling at her cleavage<sup id="cite_ref-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup> and has used his own <a href="/wiki/Fuku_Fuku_no_Mi" title="Fuku Fuku no Mi">Fuku Fuku no Mi</a> to manifest revealing outfits for her to wear.<sup id="cite_ref-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup> He showed his anger and jealousy at Momonosuke bathing with Robin and sleeping in the same bed with the women of the Straw Hat Pirates.<sup id="cite_ref-c699_24-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c699-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup> 
</p><p>Since Oden's and <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Toki" title="Kouzuki Toki">Kouzuki Toki</a>'s deaths, Kin'emon now dutifully serves <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Momonosuke" title="Kouzuki Momonosuke">Kouzuki Momonosuke</a>, heir to the <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Family" title="Kouzuki Family">Kouzuki Family</a>, protecting him from any harm or threat. Kin'emon cares deeply for Momonosuke, traveling to the dangerous Punk Hazard island<sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup> and challenging the <a href="/wiki/Seven_Warlords_of_the_Sea" title="Seven Warlords of the Sea">Warlord of the Sea</a> <a href="/wiki/Trafalgar_D._Water_Law" title="Trafalgar D. Water Law">Trafalgar Law</a> in order to find his young master. Even after being chopped to pieces, Kin'emon's torso and legs still attempted to search for Momonosuke and attacked anything that got in the way. When Kin'emon learned that Momonosuke could have been left behind during an escape sequence, he recklessly rushed through a mass of <a href="/wiki/Shinokuni" title="Shinokuni">deadly gas</a> just to rescue him, with little regard for his own safety as a demonstration of fierce loyalty.<sup id="cite_ref-c690_28-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c690-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>By his own admittance, Kin'emon is the type of person who does not give up easily when it comes to a certain matter. He was adamant in making <a href="/wiki/Ashura_Doji" title="Ashura Doji">Ashura Doji</a> their ally once again, despite the bandit's initial refusal to join Kin'emon's cause.<sup id="cite_ref-c925_29-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c925-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup> To this end, Kin'emon was not above framing him for stealing from the Beasts Pirates. However, after being confronted by Ashura, Kin'emon realized this error and that he was ignorant of the suffering his comrade had endured for the last 20 years. As the leader of the <a href="/wiki/Nine_Red_Scabbards" title="Nine Red Scabbards">Nine Red Scabbards</a>, Kin'emon knows how to take charge in times of war and rally his soldiers to victory. Still, he may think of himself as smarter than he truly is, which can lead to embarrassing situations as others praise his accidental leadership and strategic feats. 
</p><p>Kin'emon seems to have no knowledge of Devil Fruits, which he considers a form of sorcery (including his own). The same applies for stranger, unusual abilities, classifying them as either ninjutsu or the work of a creature from folklore. He is also unaware of other modern things that are commonplace outside Wano, including dishes like pizza.<sup id="cite_ref-c699_24-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c699-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Relationships">Relationships</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKin%2527emon%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D7&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Family">Family</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKin%2527emon%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D8&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Tsurujo">Tsurujo</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKin%2527emon%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D9&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Kin'emon is <a href="/wiki/Marriage" title="Marriage">married</a> to a woman from <a href="/wiki/Wano_Country" title="Wano Country">Wano Country</a> called <a href="/wiki/Tsurujo" title="Tsurujo">Tsurujo</a>. They have known each other since childhood. During their younger years, Tsurujo would threaten Kin'emon if he tried taking her money, but she did it to make him change his ways. She was deeply concerned with Kin'emon's well-being, begging him to quit living as a thug and find a normal job, becoming upset when Kin'emon disregarded her advice by claiming that no one would care if he were to die. 
</p><p>During the <a href="/wiki/Mountain_God_Incident" title="Mountain God Incident">Mountain God Incident</a>, once Kin'emon learned that Tsurujo had been devoured by the Mountain God, he remembered all the times Tsurujo stood up for him and paid for his antics, furiously attacking the beast so it would release her and showing no concern for his own life if Tsurujo were to die.<sup id="cite_ref-c961p5-9_18-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c961p5-9-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Even after being separated for 20 years, Kin'emon is still loyal to Tsurujo and was relieved to hear about her safety from Kikunojo.<sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> Tsurujo herself is faithful to her husband, never once losing hope that he would return someday even after 20 years, as evidenced by the fact she did not seek another husband. Kin'emon was concerned for her well-being when Kaidou started rampaging around <a href="/wiki/Kuri" title="Kuri">Kuri</a>, rushing to her rescue once he learned about her presence at <a href="/wiki/Kuri#Okobore_Town" title="Kuri">Okobore Town</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup> Kin'emon was happy to see Tsurujo again from afar, though restrained himself from reuniting with her because it was not the appropriate time.<sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup> During the start of the raid to <a href="/wiki/Onigashima" title="Onigashima">Onigashima</a>, Kin'emon ended up learning about Okobore Town being razed to the ground by <a href="/wiki/Holed%27em" title="Holed&#39;em">Holed'em</a> and expressed sorrow and despair. After the raid on Onigashima, Kin'emon reunited with his wife and they both celebrated.<sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Kouzuki_Family">Kouzuki Family</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKin%2527emon%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D10&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Kouzuki_Oden">Kouzuki Oden</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKin%2527emon%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D11&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Kin'emon held absolute admiration and respect for <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Oden" title="Kouzuki Oden">Kouzuki Oden</a>, the daimyo of <a href="/wiki/Kuri" title="Kuri">Kuri</a>. It began with the <a href="/wiki/Mountain_God_Incident" title="Mountain God Incident">Mountain God Incident</a> that caused destruction at the Flower Capital. When Oden defeated the <a href="/wiki/Mountain_God" title="Mountain God">Mountain God</a>, he saved Kin'emon's childhood friend Tsurujo in the process and also took the blame for the beast's rampage. This convinced Kin'emon to dedicate his life to Oden. His loyalty to his lord was so immense that he and the other retainers attempted to steal money from another daimyo, <a href="/wiki/Shimotsuki_Yasuie" title="Shimotsuki Yasuie">Shimotsuki Yasuie</a>, in order to support Oden, who was facing financial difficulties at the time. 
</p><p>That being said, Kin'emon disliked Oden's insistence in trying to sail away from Wano. When the <a href="/wiki/Whitebeard_Pirates" title="Whitebeard Pirates">Whitebeard Pirates</a> landed in the country, Kin'emon seemingly knew his lord well enough to suspect he was trying to leave with the pirates instead of driving them off the country,<sup id="cite_ref-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup> and panicked when Oden indeed attempted to sneak away with the future Emperor.<sup id="cite_ref-c964p2-3_35-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c964p2-3-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup> Years later, when Oden returned to the country as one of the <a href="/wiki/Roger_Pirates" title="Roger Pirates">Roger Pirates</a>, he remained resolute in his desire to finish Roger's quest in spite of their imploring, which elicited a rude response from Kin'emon and the other Scabbards.<sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Kin'emon cared dearly for his master and was deeply saddened by his brutal execution at the hands of the Beasts Pirates, being constantly driven to tears when he recalled Oden's demise in spite of his samurai pride. Alongside his fellow retainers, Kin'emon is willing to risk his life to avenge Oden and fulfill his last wish, which is to open the borders of <a href="/wiki/Wano_Country" title="Wano Country">Wano Country</a>. When Oden was alive, Kin'emon refused his offer to teach his personal swordsmanship style out of absolute respect. During the Scabbards' decisive confrontation against Kaidou during the Fire Festival, Kin'emon decided to imitate his master's swordsmanship to honor him, and succeeded in performing his most powerful technique on Kaidou.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Kouzuki_Momonosuke">Kouzuki Momonosuke</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKin%2527emon%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D12&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Momonosuke" title="Kouzuki Momonosuke">Momonosuke</a> is his master's son and the heir of the <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Family" title="Kouzuki Family">Kouzuki Family</a>. As a loyal retainer of the Kouzuki Family, Kin'emon cares deeply for him and always shows massive concern for his well-being; he traveled to <a href="/wiki/Punk_Hazard" title="Punk Hazard">Punk Hazard</a>, challenged <a href="/wiki/Trafalgar_D._Water_Law" title="Trafalgar D. Water Law">Trafalgar Law</a>, a <a href="/wiki/Seven_Warlords_of_the_Sea" title="Seven Warlords of the Sea">Warlord of the Sea</a> and braved through a cloud of deadly poisonous gas to rescue his young master after they got accidentally separated. They both pretended to be father and son in order to protect Momonosuke's identity, so the boy would not be targeted by their enemies, the <a href="/wiki/Donquixote_Pirates" title="Donquixote Pirates">Donquixote Pirates</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Beasts_Pirates" title="Beasts Pirates">Beasts Pirates</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c817_38-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c817-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup> Despite stating that he detests dragons, Kin'emon's staunchness for his young lord was greater, not rejecting Momonosuke for being able to turn into a dragon. At Zou, Kin'emon recognized that Momonosuke, despite his young age, did not want to be treated as a child and was glad that Luffy thought of the youngster as an equal.
</p><p>Despite being master and servant, Kin'emon can become jealous of Momonosuke and is not afraid of reprimanding him for his perverted antics. After finding out that Momonosuke was bathing with <a href="/wiki/Nico_Robin" title="Nico Robin">Nico Robin</a>, he became enraged towards the young lord, telling him to cut off his topknot as repentance, proclaiming him as the worst kid, and cursing him out in his thoughts.<sup id="cite_ref-c699_24-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c699-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup> Although the two were not related,<sup id="cite_ref-c817p8_14-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c817p8-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> the <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">Straw Hat Pirates</a> noted that they both looked alike and shared the same perverted traits, which made the lie about being father and son believable.<sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Kouzuki_Hiyori">Kouzuki Hiyori</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKin%2527emon%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D13&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>As the daughter of his master, Oden, Kin'emon naturally cares for the welfare of <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Hiyori" title="Kouzuki Hiyori">Kouzuki Hiyori</a>, Momonosuke's younger sister.
</p><p>Kin'emon learned about Hiyori being alive from Kawamatsu, feeling tearful relief as he had just assumed the worst due to Kawamatsu's capture. He was even more surprised to learn that Hiyori had grown from a misbehaving tomboy into a well-mannered lady.<sup id="cite_ref-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Friends_and_Allies">Friends and Allies</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKin%2527emon%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D14&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Denjiro">Denjiro</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKin%2527emon%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D15&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Out of the fellow members of the Nine Red Scabbards, Kin'emon has known <a href="/wiki/Denjiro" title="Denjiro">Denjiro</a> the longest, having been close friends even before meeting Oden. When Kin'emon recklessly attacked the Mountain God for swallowing Tsurujo, Denjiro expressed great worry, telling him to stop endangering his life. Like Denjiro, Kin'emon shared his immense admiration for Oden and pledged to serve him together. Kin'emon also had the utmost respect for Denjiro's strength, believing him to be a powerful ally for the Kouzuki Family's revolution to overthrow Orochi. He had full faith that Denjiro was still alive after 20 years and was sure that he would join them in the final battle.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 200px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/3d/Denjiro%27s_Blind_Admiration_of_Kin%27emon.png/revision/latest?cb=20211012053557" class="image"><img alt="Denjiro&#39;s Blind Admiration of Kin&#39;emon" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="113" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Denjiro&#39;s Blind Admiration of Kin&#39;emon.png" data-image-key="Denjiro%27s_Blind_Admiration_of_Kin%27emon.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/3d/Denjiro%27s_Blind_Admiration_of_Kin%27emon.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20211012053557" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/3d/Denjiro%27s_Blind_Admiration_of_Kin%27emon.png/revision/latest?cb=20211012053557" class="image"><img alt="Denjiro&#39;s Blind Admiration of Kin&#39;emon" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/3d/Denjiro%27s_Blind_Admiration_of_Kin%27emon.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20211012053557" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="113" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Denjiro&#39;s Blind Admiration of Kin&#39;emon.png" data-image-key="Denjiro%27s_Blind_Admiration_of_Kin%27emon.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/3d/Denjiro%27s_Blind_Admiration_of_Kin%27emon.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20211012053557" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Denjiro%27s_Blind_Admiration_of_Kin%27emon.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Denjiro's blind admiration for Kin'emon.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Indeed, when they met again for the raid on <a href="/wiki/Onigashima" title="Onigashima">Onigashima</a>, Kin'emon was surprised to see Denjiro again once the latter discarded his guise as Kyoshiro. Denjiro took advantage of Orochi's trust and joined Kin'emon after freeing the imprisoned rebels in the Flower Capital. Denjiro blindly looks up to Kin'emon and admires his craftiness and leadership skills to the point of not realizing that those tend to be a result of Kin'emon's dumb luck.<sup id="cite_ref-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup><br style="clear:both;" />
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Raizo">Raizo</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKin%2527emon%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D16&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><a href="/wiki/Raizo" title="Raizo">Raizo</a> is a ninja and Kin'emon's comrade. He accompanied Kin'emon, Momonosuke, and Kanjuro on their journey to <a href="/wiki/Zou" title="Zou">Zou</a>, but got shipwrecked and separated due to their lack of sailing skills. He and Kanjuro were relieved when the Minks reassured them that Raizo was safe and later happily reunited with the ninja.
</p><p>Unlike Denjiro, Raizo correctly guessed that Kin'emon misunderstood Yasuie's message, and while he was not angry at his leader due to it working out in their favor, he was annoyed that Kin'emon refused to admit it.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inuarashi_and_Nekomamushi">Inuarashi and Nekomamushi</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKin%2527emon%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D17&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>When Oden first brought <a href="/wiki/Inuarashi" title="Inuarashi">Inuarashi</a>, <a href="/wiki/Nekomamushi" title="Nekomamushi">Nekomamushi</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Kawamatsu" title="Kawamatsu">Kawamatsu</a> to Kuri Castle, Kin'emon was shocked and surprised at the sight of talking animals, and even questioned his lord about why he would let what were considered to be monsters to enter their domain. 
</p><p>However, as fellow retainers of Oden, Kin'emon views the two minks as trustworthy comrades. In fact, when Kin'emon's group left Wano after traveling through time, their first move was to head to Zou, the homeland of Inuarashi and Nekomamushi, in hopes of finding help for their revolution (following Oden's advice that the <a href="/wiki/Mink_Tribe" title="Mink Tribe">Mink Tribe</a> were the biggest allies the <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Family" title="Kouzuki Family">Kouzuki Family</a> had). Upon reuniting with the two minks, Kin'emon commented that he was happy to discover they were alive and later cried once he found out about the extent of the destruction the Mink Tribe endured for Raizo's safety.<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Unlike Denjiro, Inuarashi correctly guessed that Kin'emon misunderstood Yasuie's message, and while he was not angry at his leader due to it working out in their favor, he was annoyed that Kin'emon refused to admit it.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Kikunojo">Kikunojo</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKin%2527emon%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D18&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>They appear to be on good terms, as <a href="/wiki/Kikunojo" title="Kikunojo">Kikunojo</a> respectfully refers to Kin'emon as Kin-sama. Kin'emon trusted Kikunojo to keep watch of the enemy as he, Kanjuro, Raizo and Momonosuke left the country. After a long period of separation, Kikunojo was so overjoyed to see Kin'emon again that she tightly hugged him on sight and blushed in his presence, making him uncomfortable (something Sanji compared to flirting). Kikunojo stayed under <a href="/wiki/Tsurujo" title="Tsurujo">Tsurujo</a>'s employment while Kin'emon was absent, updating her comrade about his wife's well-being.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Ashura_Doji">Ashura Doji</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKin%2527emon%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D19&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>As fellow followers of Oden, Kin'emon has tremendous respect for <a href="/wiki/Ashura_Doji" title="Ashura Doji">Ashura Doji</a>'s strength, believing that he was the equivalent of a hundred men and an invaluable asset in their revolution against Orochi and Kaidou. However, when Ashura (under the alias of Shutenmaru) reunited with Kin'emon, the bandit leader rejected rejoining their campaign to overthrow Kaidou and Orochi, stating that he did not share the same loyalty the Red Scabbards held for the Kouzuki Family since he only admired Kouzuki Oden. He became disillusioned with Kin'emon and the others for vanishing for 20 years, having lost several of his subordinates to Kaidou.
</p><p>Regardless, Kin'emon refused to give up and tried to force Ashura to become their ally by framing him for theft. However, Ashura became even angrier after discovering what Kin'emon had done, but was still lenient enough to listen to Kin'emon's apology and pleas due to Yasuie's execution. Ashura then showed Kin'emon and <a href="/wiki/Inuarashi" title="Inuarashi">Inuarashi</a> the graves of his fallen comrades, explaining the fate of their allies after they had lost patience in waiting for their return. Ashura then decided to rejoin his former team, taking on a friendlier attitude towards Kin'emon.
</p><p>Unlike Denjiro, Ashura correctly guessed that Kin'emon misunderstood Yasuie's message, and while he was not angry at his leader due to it working out in their favor, he was annoyed that Kin'emon refused to admit it.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Kawamatsu">Kawamatsu</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKin%2527emon%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D20&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>When Oden first brought <a href="/wiki/Kawamatsu" title="Kawamatsu">Kawamatsu</a>, along with <a href="/wiki/Inuarashi" title="Inuarashi">Inuarashi</a> and <a href="/wiki/Nekomamushi" title="Nekomamushi">Nekomamushi</a>, to Kuri Castle, Kin'emon was just as shocked and surprised at the sight of the young <a href="/wiki/Fish-Men" title="Fish-Men">fish-man</a> as he did to the talking dog and cat. However, as fellow retainers of Oden, Kin'emon views Kawamatsu as a true companion, comparing his strength to that of a hundred men. Kin'emon also felt sympathy to hearing his plight as an orphan.
</p><p>In fact, when Kin'emon spoke to him after 20 years, he was more than happy to learn he was still alive and kicking. The comrades soon reunited and were pleased to see each other after so long. Unlike Denjiro, Kawamatsu correctly guessed that Kin'emon misunderstood Yasuie's message, and while he was not angry at his leader due to it working out in their favor, he was annoyed that Kin'emon refused to admit it.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Shinobu">Shinobu</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKin%2527emon%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D21&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><a href="/wiki/Shinobu" title="Shinobu">Shinobu</a> considers herself Kin'emon's protégée. She contributed to the Red Scabbards' escape after the events of the <a href="/wiki/Legendary_Hour" title="Legendary Hour">Legendary Hour</a>, much to Kin'emon's appreciation. Saddened by Oden's sacrifice and death, Shinobu asked Kin'emon if she could become a retainer of Oden, to which the Scabbard leader did not object.<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Straw_Hat_Pirates">Straw Hat Pirates</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKin%2527emon%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D22&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Even though he initially scorned them after finding out that they were pirates (having stated his strong dislike for them), Kin'emon started to view the <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">Straw Hat Pirates</a> as different from most. However, despite knowing this, he was not willing to break his pride and ask for their help at first. As they further adventured together, Kin'emon came to view the Straw Hats as his biggest allies to free Wano, and by the time they reached his homeland, Kin'emon had become friendly enough to tell them his whole background, as well as share various stories about his late master, Kouzuki Oden.<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Kin'emon and Sanji have an interesting relationship, as the Straw Hat cook took pity of Kin'emon's situation as a helpless severed head and decided to bring him along, despite frequently bickering with the samurai. Kin'emon was too proud to beg for help, but at the same time did not repudiate Sanji's uncalled kindness, pushing his luck too far at one point (which earned him a beating). After nearly freezing to death when his torso fell into a frozen lake, Kin'emon finally forsook his pride and gratefully accepted his aid. When Sanji saved his torso from being eaten by sharks, he bowed to and thanked him, stating that he was now in debt.<sup id="cite_ref-c672_21-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c672-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> Kin'emon has since come to greatly respect and trust the Straw Hats, immediately choosing to eat Sanji's food and telling his "son" Momonosuke that they were legitimate allies.
When Sanji was <a href="/wiki/Whole_Cake_Island_Arc" title="Whole Cake Island Arc">kidnapped</a> by the <a href="/wiki/Big_Mom_Pirates" title="Big Mom Pirates">Big Mom Pirates</a>, Kin'emon wished to join the <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">Sanji Retrieval Team</a> but couldn't due to his obligations in <a href="/wiki/Wano_Country_Arc" title="Wano Country Arc">Wano Country</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p><a href="/wiki/Roronoa_Zoro" title="Roronoa Zoro">Zoro</a> and <a href="/wiki/Brook" title="Brook">Brook</a> have developed a respectful attitude towards the samurai as not only are they all <a href="/wiki/Swordsman" title="Swordsman">swordsmen</a> of honor, but also due to Kin'emon's very own skill and <a href="/wiki/Foxfire_Style" title="Foxfire Style">fighting style</a>, of which Zoro shows interest in learning about. The three of them work quite well together in combat, being described as a "reliable trio of musketeers" by <a href="/wiki/Usopp" title="Usopp">Usopp</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c672_21-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c672-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Kin'emon has a somewhat sexist opinion on women. Having been raised in the Land of Wano, he expects women to be modest and quiet. Nami's behavior, being the complete opposite to what he is used to, comes as a reality shock to him. Kin'emon looked down on the females around him, referring to Nami and Robin as "breast-banded lady" and "courtesan" respectively. Due to Kin'emon's perversion, he attempted to give the women promiscuous outfits when disguises for them were needed.<sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup> Nami often beats up Kin'emon for his lecherous attempts, not unlike how she usually does to <a href="/wiki/Sanji" title="Sanji">Sanji</a>.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Monkey_D._Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKin%2527emon%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D23&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" style="width:100%; clear:both;">
</table><table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" align="center" style="background:none; text-align:center;">
 <tbody><tr>
  <td style="vertical-align:top; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:&#39;Times New Roman&#39;,serif; font-weight:bold; padding:.3em 0em 0em 0em; text-shadow: 1px -1px gray;">“</td>
  <td style="padding:1em 1em; font-family:&#39;Times New Roman&#39;,serif;; font-style:italic; font-size:medium; color:inherit;">Luffy-dono is different from all of you!! He is the man who will stand at the top of the seas one day!!! Even if we were to die, he will be there in our place. The dawn will come to Wano Country!!</td>
  <td style="vertical-align:bottom; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:&#39;Times New Roman&#39;,serif; font-weight:bold; padding-bottom:0em; padding-left:0em; padding-right:0em; text-shadow: -1px 1px gray;">”</td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>
<table style="padding-right: 2%; font-size:80%; text-align:right; width:100%;">
 <tbody><tr valign="top">
  <td><cite style="font-family:&#39;Arial&#39;,sans-serif;">—&#160;Kin'emon's faith in Luffy.<sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup></cite>
  </td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>

<p><br />
<a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</a> technically first met Kin'emon after defeating the <a href="/wiki/Dragon_Number_Thirteen" title="Dragon Number Thirteen">Punk Hazard dragon</a>. Kin'emon's legs were stuck to the dragon's skin, which piqued Luffy's curiosity. Luffy was so impressed by the pair of talking legs that he wished to have them join his crew, constantly playing "centaur" by sticking them to his back. After the events of Punk Hazard, Luffy let Kin'emon and Momonosuke travel with them to <a href="/wiki/Dressrosa" title="Dressrosa">Dressrosa</a> in order to search for their comrade <a href="/wiki/Kurozumi_Kanjuro" title="Kurozumi Kanjuro">Kanjuro</a>. Kin'emon assisted Luffy throughout the <a href="/wiki/Dressrosa_Arc" title="Dressrosa Arc">Dressrosa Arc</a> in various ways, from providing disguises to helping push against the string birdcage summoned by Doflamingo that threatened the whole country.
</p><p>Upon realizing they shared desire to defeat Kaidou, Kin'emon requested Luffy to allow the samurai to join their alliance, showing that his trust for the crew had increased. Kin'emon was glad that Luffy viewed Momonosuke not as an important child, but as the leader of a group of great warriors. When the <a href="/wiki/Nine_Red_Scabbards" title="Nine Red Scabbards">Nine Red Scabbards</a> assaulted Kaidou at <a href="/wiki/Onigashima" title="Onigashima">Onigashima</a>, Kin'emon affirmed his utmost faith on Luffy defeating Kaidou in their place should they fail to do so, declaring that the Straw Hat captain would in fact become Pirate King someday. After being defeated by Kaidou, Kin'emon begged Luffy to save Wano in their place, which the young pirate vowed to do as it was his friend's country.
</p><p>After Kaidou's defeat Luffy showed his respect and gratitude when he told Kin'emon he was welcome to join his crew if he ever decides to become a pirate.<sup id="cite_ref-50" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Roronoa_Zoro">Roronoa Zoro</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKin%2527emon%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D24&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>After the Punk Hazard incident, Kin'emon developed some hostility towards Zoro after noticing that he held the sword <a href="/wiki/Shusui" title="Shusui">Shusui</a>, a sacred treasure from his homeland. He wrongly believed that Zoro was the one who had desecrated <a href="/wiki/Shimotsuki_Ryuma" title="Shimotsuki Ryuma">Ryuma</a>'s grave years ago (when in truth, that was <a href="/wiki/Gecko_Moria" title="Gecko Moria">Gecko Moria</a>'s doing). He intended to challenge Zoro to a duel after their mission was complete so he could take the blade to its rightful place at <a href="/wiki/Wano_Country" title="Wano Country">Wano Country</a>. However, Kin'emon did praise Zoro for his victory against <a href="/wiki/Pica" title="Pica">Pica</a> and aided the pirate against the <a href="/wiki/Ito_Ito_no_Mi" title="Ito Ito no Mi">birdcage</a> during the climactic moments of the <a href="/wiki/Dressrosa_Arc" title="Dressrosa Arc">Dressrosa Arc</a>. 
</p><p>Kin'emon eventually gave up all his hostility and resentment after seeing how honorable Zoro is and greatly admires his strength and skill. Likewise, Kin'emon agreed to Hiyori's decision to give up one of Oden's <a href="/wiki/Meito" title="Meito">Meito</a> heirlooms, <a href="/wiki/Enma" title="Enma">Enma</a>, to Zoro in exchange for Shusui, but not before warning the Straw Hat about the extreme difficulty in handling Oden's blade.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Trafalgar_Law">Trafalgar Law</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKin%2527emon%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D25&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Kin'emon seemed to curse the <a href="/wiki/Trafalgar_D._Water_Law" title="Trafalgar D. Water Law">Warlord of the Sea</a> for separating his body parts when he came to Punk Hazard to rescue his "son" <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Momonosuke" title="Kouzuki Momonosuke">Momonosuke</a>.
</p><p>However, he apparently decided to forget his grudge and temporarily cooperated with him to defeat Caesar Clown. Afterwards, he seems to have completely gotten over it, as they traveled to Dressrosa. 
</p><p>Kin'emon even showed concern for Law when he was shot by <a href="/wiki/Donquixote_Doflamingo" title="Donquixote Doflamingo">Donquixote Doflamingo</a> and attempted to save him from the clutches of both <a href="/wiki/Issho" title="Issho">Issho</a> and Doflamingo.
</p><p>With the formation of the <a href="/wiki/Ninja-Pirate-Mink-Samurai_Alliance" title="Ninja-Pirate-Mink-Samurai Alliance">Ninja-Pirate-Mink-Samurai Alliance</a>, Kin'emon now considers Law, alongside the Straw Hat Pirates, a comrade with a shared goal of defeating <a href="/wiki/Kaidou" title="Kaidou">Kaidou</a>.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Shimotsuki_Yasuie">Shimotsuki Yasuie</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKin%2527emon%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D26&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Kin'emon held immense respect for Yasuie, not only for being one of Oden's greatest allies, but also for his past generosity in the sponsorship of grooming him and his fellow members of the Nine Red Scabbards into fully fledged samurais. Kin'emon took to heart Yasuie's advice and completely changed his brash and vulgar ways. 
</p><p>Even after 20 years, Yasuie still had complete trust in Kin'emon and his friends. When he came across the secret message Kin'emon was spreading through the country, Yasuie showed his willingness to join him.<sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> Once the meaning of the message leaked and Orochi started cracking down on the rebels, Yasuie let himself get captured so he could claim in front of the population that the message was nothing more than a prank that he had invented, saving Kin'emon's plan from failure and giving them a chance to continue the revolution. 
</p><p>Kin'emon was shocked to learn that Yasuie was still alive and tearfully expressed his gratitude for the former Hakumai daimyo's final sacrifice. Kin'emon heavily cried when witnessing Yasuie getting shot down, heartbroken by the death of his second benefactor after Oden.<sup id="cite_ref-c942_52-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c942-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> After learning that Yasuie had prepared a second rendezvous point for his allies to set sail for Onigashima in Tokage port, Kin'emon became even more determined to succeed in the Kouzuki Family's revolution, regretful that he had caused trouble for Yasuie once again and believing that it would be a major shame as a samurai to not live up to his last expectations.<sup id="cite_ref-c974_53-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c974-53">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Enemies">Enemies</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKin%2527emon%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D27&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Kaidou">Kaidou</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKin%2527emon%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D28&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
