<p>Because of his role in the Kouzuki Family's downfall, killing Kouzuki Oden and turning Wano into an industrialized wasteland, Kaidou is Kin'emon's archnemesis and the reason for his hatred of dragons. After hearing that Luffy and Law's <a href="/wiki/Pirate_Alliance" title="Pirate Alliance">Pirate Alliance</a> were targeting him, Kin'emon was horrified, but withheld his knowledge about him. 
</p><p>Kaidou initially held interest in Kin'emon and the Red Scabbards due to the possibility of them knowing something about <a href="/wiki/Laugh_Tale" title="Laugh Tale">Laugh Tale</a> from Oden, only to later learn they knew nothing. During his confrontation with the Scabbards at <a href="/wiki/Onigashima" title="Onigashima">Onigashima</a>, Kaidou admitted he had overlooked Kin'emon and the Scabbards' threat since he had never expected them to join forces with pirates. He tried to disencourage the Scabbards by citing the treacherous nature of pirates, but Kin'emon dismissed Kaidou's words, responding that Luffy would outlive the <a href="/wiki/Four_Emperors" title="Four Emperors">Emperor</a> and become Pirate King.
</p><p>While Kaidou considered Kin'emon and his fellow Scabbards to be inferior to Oden in terms of strength, he expressed admiration for their courage and unwavering resolve, and decided to personally kill them as a sign of respect. Kin'emon expressed disdain in response, claiming that dying at his hands would bring only dishonor.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Kurozumi_Orochi">Kurozumi Orochi</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKin%2527emon%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D29&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Kin'emon harbors great hatred for Orochi due to the latter collaborating with Kaidou to execute <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Oden" title="Kouzuki Oden">Kouzuki Oden</a> and bringing ruination to Wano Country by setting up countless weapon factories, causing immense industrial pollution to its regions, and monopolizing food supply for himself and the Beasts Pirates. Kin'emon vows to overthrow the shogun to avenge Oden and fulfill his dream of opening Wano. 
</p><p>Orochi deathly feared Kin'emon and the Scabbards, due to his belief and paranoia about <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Toki" title="Kouzuki Toki">Kouzuki Toki</a>'s prophecy involving the retainers of Oden overthrowing him and Kaidou. As such, Orochi ruthlessly hunted after them, with the intent of defying her foretelling.
</p><p>During the Kouzuki revolution on Onigashima, Kin'emon met Orochi face to face for the first time in twenty years, Orochi underestimating the Nine Red Scabbards from their heavy injuries from Kaidou attempted to kill them himself, Kin'emon and his fellow samurais ruthlessly decapitated all of Orochi's head, telling the dead tyrant shogun, they do not have time to deal with him, he will face judgment for all his sins in Wano in hell.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Kurozumi_Kanjuro">Kurozumi Kanjuro</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKin%2527emon%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D30&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/67/Kinemon_Pays_His_Respect_to_Kanjuro.png/revision/latest?cb=20200805225435" class="image"><img alt="Kinemon Pays His Respect to Kanjuro" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="103" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Kinemon Pays His Respect to Kanjuro.png" data-image-key="Kinemon_Pays_His_Respect_to_Kanjuro.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/67/Kinemon_Pays_His_Respect_to_Kanjuro.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20200805225435" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/67/Kinemon_Pays_His_Respect_to_Kanjuro.png/revision/latest?cb=20200805225435" class="image"><img alt="Kinemon Pays His Respect to Kanjuro" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/67/Kinemon_Pays_His_Respect_to_Kanjuro.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20200805225435" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="103" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Kinemon Pays His Respect to Kanjuro.png" data-image-key="Kinemon_Pays_His_Respect_to_Kanjuro.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/67/Kinemon_Pays_His_Respect_to_Kanjuro.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20200805225435" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Kinemon_Pays_His_Respect_to_Kanjuro.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Even after Kanjuro's betrayal, Kin'emon still pays respect to him.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Kin'emon once believed <a href="/wiki/Kurozumi_Kanjuro" title="Kurozumi Kanjuro">Kanjuro</a> to be one of his most trusted friends and allies. At Dressrosa, Kanjuro left himself behind to let Kin'emon and Momonosuke escape to <a href="/wiki/Punk_Hazard" title="Punk Hazard">Punk Hazard</a>. Upon Kin'emon's return, he prioritized Kanjuro's rescue over everything else, looking for leads about his whereabouts and searching everywhere for his comrade. Kin'emon was tearfully overjoyed to be reunited with his peer after finding him.
</p><p>Kanjuro, however, was not who Kin'emon thought he was, being in fact a spy of Orochi. After all their time spent together, Kin'emon never suspected Kanjuro to be a traitor and was shocked at the revelation. Kanjuro admitted that he did not harbor hatred for either Kin'emon or his peers, but fed Orochi continuous information about their strategies and whereabouts as early as 30 years ago, when Kuri was reformed. Kin'emon became murderous towards the traitor and attempted to behead him only to fail.<sup id="cite_ref-c974_53-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c974-53">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup> Upon seeing Kanjuro's true mastery in painting that contradicts the atrocious scribbles he contributed to the Kouzuki Family, Kin'emon expressed more hate for his former friend's extensive deception.<sup id="cite_ref-c976_54-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c976-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After Kanjuro's defeat, Kin'emon only looked upon the traitor with a sullen expression while reminiscing their time together as companions. Despite being enemies, Kin'emon still paid his respects to his former comrade and left his kasa behind, over Kanjuro's body.<sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>However, while their sentiments led them to spare Kanjuro, Kanjuro did not return such feelings, as he went onto creating a clone of Kouzuki Oden and acted out his personality with such astounding success it caught the Scabbards off guard. This act of cruelty led to Ashura suffering from a devastating explosion, which turned Kin'emon into a murderous rage.<sup id="cite_ref-c1008_56-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1008-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup> Despite so, and even after Kanjuro attempted a second time to disguise as Oden, which led the Kiku to once again drop her guard as she could not bring herself to harm their savior despite knowing it was a fake, Kin'emon still shed tears when he was forced to strike down Kanjuro a second time.<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Donquixote_Doflamingo">Donquixote Doflamingo</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKin%2527emon%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D31&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Kin'emon considered Doflamingo an enemy due to his role in pursuing him, Kanjuro and Momonosuke after they got stranded at Dressrosa after fleeing from Wano and separating from Raizo. Doflamingo  had managed to capture Kanjuro (as the latter purposefully left himself behind to allow Kin'emon and Momonosuke to escape), which prompted Kin'emon to search all over Dressrosa for his friend upon his return with the Straw Hats and Law. Like several other allies, Kin'emon took part in slowing down Doflamingo's Birdcage, which contributed to the Warlord's downfall.
</p><p>Kin'emon was recognized by several of Doflamingo's subordinates, who had become familiar with him through the footage televised by <a href="/wiki/Caesar_Clown" title="Caesar Clown">Caesar Clown</a> at Punk Hazard. At a later point of the arc, Kin'emon was attacked by Doflamingo himself when the former attempted to rescue Trafalgar Law from the latter's clutches outside the <a href="/wiki/Corrida_Colosseum" title="Corrida Colosseum">Corrida Colosseum</a>. Doflamingo considered Kin'emon one of his targets after the success of <a href="/wiki/Operation_SOP" title="Operation SOP">Operation SOP</a>, branding him with a one-star rank. This meant that anyone who managed to capture the samurai would be rewarded with <span style="white-space:nowrap;"><a href="/wiki/Belly" title="Belly"><img alt="Beli" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="12" height="20" data-image-name="Beli.png" data-image-key="Beli.png" data-relevant="0" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/de/Beli.png/revision/latest?cb=20141206091723" class="lazyload" /></a></span>100,000,000.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Abilities_and_Powers">Abilities and Powers</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKin%2527emon%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D32&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>As the leader of the Nine Red Scabbards, Kin'emon has a certain degree of authority among the group. As such, he is an experienced leader who can take charge during a crisis and is capable of successfully rallying soldiers to war. The other Scabbards appear to respect Kin'emon as a leader, most notably Denjiro. By combining his power with that of three other Scabbards, he was able to seriously injure Kaidou in his <a href="/wiki/Uo_Uo_no_Mi,_Model:_Seiryu" title="Uo Uo no Mi, Model: Seiryu">dragon form</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Before becoming a proper samurai, Kin'emon was nothing more than a thug who assaulted and stole from people, but his strength and reputation were already recognized by even <a href="/wiki/Hyougoro" title="Hyougoro">Hyougoro</a>, the most prominent yakuza of the <a href="/wiki/Flower_Capital" title="Flower Capital">Flower Capital</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>One of Kin'emon's more unique capabilities is his ability to speak through farting. This was convenient since it allowed Kin'emon a certain method of communication after getting cut up by Law at <a href="/wiki/Punk_Hazard" title="Punk Hazard">Punk Hazard</a>, as his legs had been attached to a dragon's body while his head remained confined in a cell in the <a href="/wiki/Third_Research_Institute" title="Third Research Institute">Third Research Institute</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c663_60-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c663-60">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup> 
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Physical_Abilities">Physical Abilities</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKin%2527emon%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D33&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Kin'emon has an extreme amount of superhuman strength, to the point that cutting through thick steel is a trivial task for him. Towards the end of the <a href="/wiki/Dressrosa_Arc" title="Dressrosa Arc">Dressrosa Arc</a>, Kin'emon helped slow down the contraction speed of <a href="/wiki/Donquixote_Doflamingo" title="Donquixote Doflamingo">Doflamingo</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Ito_Ito_no_Mi" title="Ito Ito no Mi"><b>Torikago</b></a> by pushing against it with his Haki-infused swords. At age 15, Kin'emon challenged the gigantic boar known as the <a href="/wiki/Mountain_God" title="Mountain God">Mountain God</a>, survived its violent rampage, and injured it with his katana, making it bleed.
</p><p>He also possesses an immense endurance to pain and cold; his head alone was capable of withstanding <a href="/wiki/Sanji" title="Sanji">Sanji</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Black_Leg_Style" title="Black Leg Style">powerful kicks</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup> while his torso could endure freezing temperatures that a normal person would typically die from, not to mention the biting of a vicious shark. During the <a href="/wiki/Raid_on_Onigashima" title="Raid on Onigashima">raid on Onigashima</a>, Kin'emon managed to survive a direct hit from one of Kaidou's <a href="/wiki/Haki/Supreme_King_Haki" title="Haki/Supreme King Haki">Supreme King Haki</a>-infused attacks despite prior injuries, although he was left barely standing and unable to fight further.
</p><p>Kin'emon's body is capable of processing toxic substances that would have easily caused potentially severe illness to others. Caesar's <a href="/wiki/Shinokuni" title="Shinokuni">Shinokuni</a> also seemed to have little effect on him even after it petrified his body, as he did not receive any sort of medical treatment post-release despite coming in contact with the deadly gas. Even though the rivers, wild animals, and fish of Wano became extremely toxic as a result of the pollution from Kaidou's factories, Kin'emon regularly consumed these tainted foods with no more major side effects aside from persistent diarrhea.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Tactical_Skills">Tactical Skills</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKin%2527emon%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D34&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Noted by Orochi for his tactical intellect, Kin'emon is an extremely clever tactician, having been the one to formulate most of the strategies behind the alliance's revolution against the Emperor Kaidou. 
</p><p>At Dressrosa, Kin'emon was the one who up with the idea of disguising Zoro, Luffy, and himself as <a href="/wiki/Toys" title="Toys">toys</a> with animal costumes to get away from the Marines without drawing attention. Kin'emon was also smart enough to disguise himself as <a href="/wiki/Donquixote_Doflamingo" title="Donquixote Doflamingo">Donquixote Doflamingo</a> while searching through the Dressrosa Royal Palace, allowing him to trick <a href="/wiki/Gladius" title="Gladius">Gladius</a> without the latter suspecting him of being an intruder.<sup id="cite_ref-c740_62-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c740-62">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup> At Onigashima, Kin'emon would employ similar tactics, camouflaging the members of the <a href="/wiki/Ninja-Pirate-Mink-Samurai_Alliance" title="Ninja-Pirate-Mink-Samurai Alliance">Ninja-Pirate-Mink-Samurai Alliance</a> in uniforms of the <a href="/wiki/Beasts_Pirates" title="Beasts Pirates">Beasts Pirates</a>, allowing them to better infiltrate Kaidou's domain and assimilate among his forces while remaining undetected until the time of the confrontation. Kin'emon also made sure that every ship used by the samurai sank upon landing on Onigashima, with the intent of erasing evidence of their presence from the <a href="/wiki/Orochi_Oniwabanshu" title="Orochi Oniwabanshu">Orochi Oniwabanshu</a>.
</p><p>Kin'emon's strategies, however, are not always flawless, sometimes requiring an extraordinary amount of luck for them to come into fruition. In order to recruit <a href="/wiki/Ashura_Doji" title="Ashura Doji">Shutenmaru</a>, his former comrade and leader of the <a href="/wiki/Mt._Atama_Thieves" title="Mt. Atama Thieves">Mt. Atama Thieves</a>, Kin'emon successfully framed his group for stealing supplies from the <a href="/wiki/Beasts_Pirates" title="Beasts Pirates">Beasts Pirates</a> in order to provoke conflict between them, so Ashura would find himself forced to join the rebellion out of survival, but that ended up backfiring when Ashura discovered Kin'emon's scheme. The bandit eventually rejoined the Scabbards anyway, but mostly because of Yasuie's convenient sacrifice. Something similar happened later at the start of the Onigashima raid, where Kin'emon managed to accidentally mislead the alliance's <a href="/wiki/Kurozumi_Kanjuro" title="Kurozumi Kanjuro">traitor</a> because he turned out to be the only samurai in all of Wano to not realize the real meaning of Yasuie's secret message, having overthought its contents and expecting everybody else to have followed the same logical process he did.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Luck">Luck</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKin%2527emon%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D35&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Though not on the same level as Luffy and Zoro, Kin'emon has exceptional luck, which has worked in his favor whenever he seemed to have had the worst luck. Despite losing Raizo, Momonosuke, then Kanjuro, he managed to find his way onto Punk Hazard, where during a series of events, he ended up encountering the <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">Straw Hat Pirates</a>, after Law had severed him into pieces using his <a href="/wiki/Ope_Ope_no_Mi" title="Ope Ope no Mi">Ope Ope no Mi</a>, resulting in him earning them and the <a href="/wiki/Heart_Pirates" title="Heart Pirates">Heart Pirates</a> as allies for the Raid of Onigashima. At the peak of his luck, through Kin'emon's misreading of <a href="/wiki/Shimotsuki_Yasuie" title="Shimotsuki Yasuie">Shimotsuki Yasuie</a>'s final message to them and altering their plans, he managed to deceive Kanjurou, who turned out to be a spy and a member of the <a href="/wiki/Kurozumi_Family" title="Kurozumi Family">Kurozumi Family</a>, causing him to not only reveal his own treachery, but also managing to mislead the entire opposition in attacking the wrong location. Later on, after being stabbed in the back by Kaidou, it resulted in his lower half coming undone again, same as what happened on Punk Hazard, because Law was not the one who put him back together, allowing him to survive and inform the others, who tended to him and Kiku.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Swordsmanship">Swordsmanship</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKin%2527emon%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D36&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<dl><dd><i>Further information: <a href="/wiki/Foxfire_Style" title="Foxfire Style">Foxfire Style</a></i></dd>
<dd><i>Further information: <a href="/wiki/Oden_Two_Sword_Style" title="Oden Two Sword Style">Oden Two Sword Style</a></i></dd></dl>
<p>As the leader of the Nine Red Scabbards of Kouzuki Oden, Kin'emon is one of the most powerful samurai of Wano, noted by Orochi himself to be an incredibly strong master in <a href="/wiki/Swordsman" title="Swordsman">swordsmanship</a>. His skills are extremely versatile, able to wield either one or dual wield both his swords with incredible power and precision. Even after getting dismembered into several body parts by the Ope Ope no Mi, Kin'emon was capable of putting up a fight with his legs, recklessly attacking Luffy's party when they encountered him.<sup id="cite_ref-debut_1-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-debut-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> His torso alone was able to match <a href="/wiki/Brook" title="Brook">Brook</a> in swordsmanship, utilizing a two-sword style despite the lack of a head or legs.<sup id="cite_ref-c659_63-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c659-63">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup> Alongside Zoro and Brook, Kin'emon was able to cut down multiple G-5 Marines with great ease and is capable of cutting steel as well.<sup id="cite_ref-c677_64-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c677-64">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/0e/Foxfire_Style_Infobox.png/revision/latest?cb=20191102094851" class="image"><img alt="Foxfire Style Infobox" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="166" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Foxfire Style Infobox.png" data-image-key="Foxfire_Style_Infobox.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/0e/Foxfire_Style_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20191102094851" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/0e/Foxfire_Style_Infobox.png/revision/latest?cb=20191102094851" class="image"><img alt="Foxfire Style Infobox" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/0e/Foxfire_Style_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20191102094851" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="166" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Foxfire Style Infobox.png" data-image-key="Foxfire_Style_Infobox.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/0e/Foxfire_Style_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20191102094851" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Foxfire_Style_Infobox.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kin'emon burns some of Smiley by cutting it.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Kin'emon specializes in a sword style he calls <b>Foxfire Style</b><span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">狐火流</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Kitsunebi-ryū</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>, literally "Fox-Fire Style")</span>.<sup id="cite_ref-intro_8-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-intro-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup> He is somehow capable of generating, attacking with, and cutting fire with one of his swords. Using this, he had no problem cutting through <a href="/wiki/Smiley" title="Smiley">Smiley</a>'s pieces (which were highly flammable) and subsequently slash through the resulting explosion.<sup id="cite_ref-c672_21-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c672-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> His fire-enhanced sword slashes are powerful enough to seriously injure a dragon, despite its scales being stronger than steel. Kin'emon's mastery of this sword style was great enough to split apart even Kaidou's <b><a href="/wiki/Uo_Uo_no_Mi,_Model:_Seiryu" title="Uo Uo no Mi, Model: Seiryu">Bolo Breath</a></b> which has immense firepower.<sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup> He is also able to generate flames to safely cauterize wounds.<sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 220px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/2e/Kin%27emon_Using_Oden_Two_Sword_Style.png/revision/latest?cb=20230906071540" class="image"><img alt="Kin&#39;emon Using Oden Two Sword Style" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="220" height="124" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Kin&#39;emon Using Oden Two Sword Style.png" data-image-key="Kin%27emon_Using_Oden_Two_Sword_Style.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/2e/Kin%27emon_Using_Oden_Two_Sword_Style.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20230906071540" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/2e/Kin%27emon_Using_Oden_Two_Sword_Style.png/revision/latest?cb=20230906071540" class="image"><img alt="Kin&#39;emon Using Oden Two Sword Style" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/2e/Kin%27emon_Using_Oden_Two_Sword_Style.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20230906071540" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="220" height="124" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Kin&#39;emon Using Oden Two Sword Style.png" data-image-key="Kin%27emon_Using_Oden_Two_Sword_Style.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/2e/Kin%27emon_Using_Oden_Two_Sword_Style.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20230906071540" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Kin%27emon_Using_Oden_Two_Sword_Style.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kin'emon using Oden Two Sword Style.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Moreover, Kin'emon is capable of emulating Oden's signature <b>Oden Two Sword Style</b> style, to perform one of his techniques albeit being significantly less powerful.<sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>During his youth, Kin'emon's skills were acknowledged by Hyougoro, who stated that his subordinates could never be able to stand toe-to-toe with him. He was shown being able to fight on par with Ashura Doji during a sparring session.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Devil_Fruit">Devil Fruit</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKin%2527emon%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D37&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<dl><dd><i>Further information: <a href="/wiki/Fuku_Fuku_no_Mi" title="Fuku Fuku no Mi">Fuku Fuku no Mi</a></i></dd></dl>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9c/Fuku_Fuku_no_Mi_Infobox.png/revision/latest?cb=20181020010802" class="image"><img alt="Fuku Fuku no Mi Infobox" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Fuku Fuku no Mi Infobox.png" data-image-key="Fuku_Fuku_no_Mi_Infobox.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9c/Fuku_Fuku_no_Mi_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20181020010802" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9c/Fuku_Fuku_no_Mi_Infobox.png/revision/latest?cb=20181020010802" class="image"><img alt="Fuku Fuku no Mi Infobox" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9c/Fuku_Fuku_no_Mi_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20181020010802" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Fuku Fuku no Mi Infobox.png" data-image-key="Fuku_Fuku_no_Mi_Infobox.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9c/Fuku_Fuku_no_Mi_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20181020010802" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Fuku_Fuku_no_Mi_Infobox.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kin'emon making coats appear on the Straw Hats and the children.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Kin'emon ate the Fuku Fuku no Mi, a <a href="/wiki/Paramecia" title="Paramecia">Paramecia</a>-type <a href="/wiki/Devil_Fruit" title="Devil Fruit">Devil Fruit</a> that allows him to transform small objects placed on a person's head, such as pebbles and leaves, into various articles of clothing. The clothes disappear once they have been removed or once they have taken a certain amount of damage.<sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup> He must first visualize the appearance of the clothes, otherwise his creations are limited.<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_7-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>While this power lacks direct combat applications, it does have a number of support functions; he can provide quick disguises for himself and his allies, letting them move around enemy territory undetected. He can also provide the necessary attire for survival in harsh weather conditions, such as creating a winter coat that can be worn in a frigid climate. Finally, he can create armor that can be used in combat.
</p><p>Like many characters from Wano, Kin'emon considers his Devil Fruit ability a form of sorcery, but he is aware of his weakness to bodies of water.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Haki">Haki</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKin%2527emon%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D38&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<dl><dd><div class="noprint"><i>Main article&#58; <a href="/wiki/Haki" title="Haki">Haki</a></i></div></dd></dl>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Observation_Haki">Observation Haki</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKin%2527emon%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D39&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Kin'emon is a very skilled user of <a href="/wiki/Haki/Observation_Haki" title="Haki/Observation Haki">Observation Haki</a>, as even after getting split by Law, his legs and his torso were able to fight, dodge attacks, and even defeat people without being attached to his head. When Kin'emon's disembodied legs first "spoke", they said it could feel the "aura" of other people around it, accurately attacking them.<sup id="cite_ref-debut_1-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-debut-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> Furthermore, his separated body parts navigated through Punk Hazard's geography by sensing their surroundings (although his legs still managed to somehow get stuck to a <a href="/wiki/Dragon_Number_Thirteen" title="Dragon Number Thirteen">dragon</a>).<sup id="cite_ref-c663_60-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c663-60">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Armament_Haki">Armament Haki</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKin%2527emon%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D40&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/93/Kin%27emon_Using_Armament_Haki.png/revision/latest?cb=20160221230932" class="image"><img alt="Kin&#39;emon Using Armament Haki" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="151" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Kin&#39;emon Using Armament Haki.png" data-image-key="Kin%27emon_Using_Armament_Haki.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/93/Kin%27emon_Using_Armament_Haki.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20160221230932" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/93/Kin%27emon_Using_Armament_Haki.png/revision/latest?cb=20160221230932" class="image"><img alt="Kin&#39;emon Using Armament Haki" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/93/Kin%27emon_Using_Armament_Haki.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20160221230932" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="151" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Kin&#39;emon Using Armament Haki.png" data-image-key="Kin%27emon_Using_Armament_Haki.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/93/Kin%27emon_Using_Armament_Haki.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20160221230932" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Kin%27emon_Using_Armament_Haki.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kin'emon imbuing his swords with Armament.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Kin'emon is an extremely skilled user of <a href="/wiki/Haki/Armament_Haki" title="Haki/Armament Haki">Armament Haki</a>, known in Wano as "Ryuo".<sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup> His Armament Haki is strong enough to withstand the Torikago's razor sharp threads, which can slice cannon balls and meteorites with ease. When fueled by rage, his Haki-infused sword was able to pierce Kaidou's nigh-invulnerable body.<sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70">&#91;70&#93;</a></sup><br style="clear:both;" />
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Weapons">Weapons</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKin%2527emon%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D41&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Kin'emon wields two katana named <a href="/wiki/Sukesan_and_Kakusan" title="Sukesan and Kakusan">Sukesan and Kakusan</a> which he uses for his Foxfire Style and Oden Two Sword Style.<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_7-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>He also has a small dagger with him, although it appears that he only carries it around to commit <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Seppuku" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Seppuku">seppuku</a> if a situation calls for it.<sup id="cite_ref-c699_24-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c699-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup>
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Other_Appearances">Other Appearances</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKin%2527emon%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D48&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Other_Media">Other Media</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKin%2527emon%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D49&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 150px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/2e/Kin%27emon_Water_Battle.png/revision/latest?cb=20201218024513" class="image"><img alt="Kin&#39;emon Water Battle" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="150" height="153" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Kin&#39;emon Water Battle.png" data-image-key="Kin%27emon_Water_Battle.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/2e/Kin%27emon_Water_Battle.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20201218024513" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/2e/Kin%27emon_Water_Battle.png/revision/latest?cb=20201218024513" class="image"><img alt="Kin&#39;emon Water Battle" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/2e/Kin%27emon_Water_Battle.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20201218024513" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="150" height="153" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Kin&#39;emon Water Battle.png" data-image-key="Kin%27emon_Water_Battle.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/2e/Kin%27emon_Water_Battle.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20201218024513" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Kin%27emon_Water_Battle.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kin'emon in Water Battle 2015.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li>In <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Premier_Show#One_Piece_Premier_Show_2013" title="One Piece Premier Show">One Piece Premier Show 2013</a> and <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Premier_Show#One_Piece_Premier_Show_2014" title="One Piece Premier Show">One Piece Premier Show 2014</a>, Kin'emon and Momonosuke accompany the Straw Hat Pirates to <a href="/wiki/Paradise_Island" title="Paradise Island">Paradise Island</a> and <a href="/wiki/Madatascar_Island" title="Madatascar Island">Madatascar Island</a> respectively. In <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Premier_Show#One_Piece_Premier_Show_2015" title="One Piece Premier Show">One Piece Premier Show 2015</a>, he helps the crew fight <a href="/wiki/B%C3%BCrst_Lab" title="Bürst Lab">Bürst Lab</a> to save <a href="/wiki/Nami" title="Nami">Nami</a>.</li>
<li>Kin'emon appears in the 2015 <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Water_Battle" title="One Piece Water Battle">One Piece Water Battle</a> show.</li>
<li>Kin'emon appears in the <a href="/wiki/Nefertari_Vivi" title="Nefertari Vivi">Vivi</a> version of <a href="/wiki/Hungry_Days" title="Hungry Days">Hungry Days</a>.<br style="clear:both;" /></li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Trivia">Trivia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKin%2527emon%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D50&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>Kin'emon seems to have a fox theme, as his epithet "<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Foxfire_(disambiguation)" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Foxfire (disambiguation)">Foxfire</a>"<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">狐火</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">kitsune-bi</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span>, fighting style, and Devil Fruit ability to disguise himself and others are associated with the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kitsune#Shapeshifting" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Kitsune">kitsune</a> of Japanese folklore.</li>
<li>For his official introduction, the regular information box was replaced by a Japanese scroll with his details on it.<sup id="cite_ref-intro_8-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-intro-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup> Since then, every member of his party had the same information box variant except Momonosuke's initial, fake introduction.<sup id="cite_ref-71" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-71">&#91;71&#93;</a></sup>
<ul><li>His introduction as "Donquixote Doflaemon"<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">ドンキホーテ・ドフラえもん</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Donkihōte Dofuraemon</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span>, his Doflamingo disguise, also had the regular information box.<sup id="cite_ref-c740_62-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c740-62">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup></li></ul></li>
<li>Kin'emon's notably good luck may be a reference to his Devil Fruit, as both the kanji for clothes (服) and good fortune (福) are pronounced as "fuku".</li>
<li>Kin'emon's favorite foods are <a href="/wiki/Tsurujo" title="Tsurujo">O-Tsuru</a>'s <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Shiruko" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Shiruko">oshiruko</a><sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_7-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Daikon" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Daikon">daikon</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-sbs96_10-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-sbs96-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> and his least favorite foods are <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Udon" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Udon">tanuki udon</a> and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wine" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Wine">wine</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_7-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
<ul><li>Fittingly enough, daikon are one of the main ingredients in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Oden" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Oden">oden</a>, just as Kin'emon was one of <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Oden" title="Kouzuki Oden">Kouzuki Oden's</a> main retainers.</li></ul></li>
<li>Kin'emon's animal resemblance is a <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fox" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Fox">fox</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_7-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>Kin'emon's hobby is touring <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Teahouse" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Teahouse">teahouses</a> with O-Tsuru.<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_7-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="SBS-Based_Trivia">SBS-Based Trivia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKin%2527emon%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D51&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li>Kin'emon's birthday, January 29, comes from word "Clothes"<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">衣服</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Ifuku</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span>, a reference to his Devil Fruit's ability, since 1-2-9 can be derived from i-fu-ku.<sup id="cite_ref-birth_9-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-birth-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>Kin'emon's name was taken from Oda's favorite Japanese actor <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Yorozuya_Kinnosuke" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Yorozuya Kinnosuke">Nakamura Kinnosuke</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-72" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-72">&#91;72&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
